# Source Inventory & Ranking

Sources that need (or may eventually need) dedicated adapters. Scores are 1вҖ“5, higher is better. **Ease** = ease of integration (format cleanliness, bulk access, stability). **License** = openness/clarity (5 = CC/PD with bulk grant, 1 = restricted/unclear). Verify licenses and endpoints at implementation time вҖ” this table reflects the landscape as of mid-2026 and these projects do change terms and infrastructure.

## Tier 1 вҖ” build first (large, open, clean formats)

| # | Source | Content | Format | Size | Value | Ease | License | Notes |
|---|--------|---------|--------|:----:|:-----:|:----:|:-------:|-------|
| 1 | **PerseusDL canonical-greekLit / canonical-latinLit** | Core classical Greek & Latin literature | TEI XML (EpiDoc/CapiTainS), CTS URNs, git | 5 | 5 | 5 | 5 (CC BY-SA) | The backbone. Clean, versioned, citation scheme built in. Adapter here defines the reference implementation. **Status: LIVE (greekLit)** вҖ” first sync 2026-07-03: 744 docs / 238,525 passages, 25 quarantined (upstream `@n` gaps). **latinLit: READY** вҖ” `PerseusLatin < Perseus` shipped P7-3 (the designed one-line NAMESPACE sibling; registry `perseus-latin`, `enabled: false`), awaiting the owner-initiated first sync (multi-GB clone of canonical-latinLit) at the phase gate. |
| 2 | **OpenGreekAndLatin / First1KGreek** | Greek works not in Perseus (first 1,000 years CE) | TEI XML, CTS, git | 4 | 5 | 5 | 5 (CC BY-SA) | Same conventions as Perseus вҖ” nearly free once adapter #1 exists. **Status: LIVE** вҖ” first sync 2026-07-04: 1,054 docs / 226k passages, 37 quarantined. **P11-5: tlg0527 IS the LXX** вҖ” Swete's *Septuaginta* (1901), 55 grc book-documents already synced at verse grain (chapter.verse CTS urns) + ~40 Brenton eng translations; it is the alignment hub's `ot`-work Greek witness via the `cts-verse` extractor (registry-only, zero new code вҖ” see #44 for why Rahlfs is not ingestable). |
| 3 | **PROIEL treebanks** | Gothic (Wulfila), OCS Codex Marianus, Greek NT, Classical Armenian, Latin вҖ” fully lemmatized/parsed | PROIEL XML, git | 3 | 5 | 4 | 5 (CC BY-NC-SA) | Highest linguistic value per byte for comparative IE work. NC clause: record it. **Status: LIVE** вҖ” first sync 2026-07-04: 12 docs (release 20180408, frozen), 0 quarantined. |
| 4 | **Universal Dependencies (ancient treebanks)** | Ancient Greek, Latin, OCS, Old East Slavic, Vedic Sanskrit, Gothic, Coptic, Classical Chinese | CoNLL-U, git | 4 | 5 | 5 | 4вҖ“5 (mostly CC) | One parser handles a dozen languages. Overlaps PROIEL (TOROT/PROIEL data appear here too) вҖ” dedupe by document ID. **Status: LIVE** вҖ” first sync 2026-07-04: 4 treebanks / 12 docs, 0 quarantined. **P10-2 (Slavic expansion, shipped):** the `TREEBANKS` map grew to **6 treebanks** (now **7** with P13-1b below) вҖ” gothic-proiel, greek-proiel, sanskrit-vedic, latin-ittb, plus **`old-east-slavic-birchbark`** + **`old-east-slavic-rnc`** (both `CC BY-SA 4.0`, verified in each repo's README/LICENSE at fixture time 2026-07-09; language `orv`; genuinely-new vernacular/Middle-Russian OES, no PROIEL/TOROT overlap). Config+fixture change, no new family. The `chu-PROIEL`/`orv-TOROT` UD conversions are deliberately **excluded** (they re-load the native PROIEL/TOROT already synced), pinned by a dedup-guard test. Re-sync owner-fired at the phase gate. See `.docs/surveys/slavic-survey.md`. **P11-1: no Old English treebank exists in UD** (verified against the org repo list вҖ” the hoped-for config-only OE add is unavailable; watch releases). **P10-4 (split licensing):** the source class stays `nc` (most-restrictive present, correct for the PROIEL-derived treebanks) but the two Old East Slavic treebanks (birchbark, rnc) are attribution-class вҶ’ carried as a per-document `license_class: attribution` via `documents.license_override` (adapter `TREEBANKS` map вҶ’ `Document#license_override` вҶ’ loader, a metadata-only relabel: no revision bump, `content_sha256` untouched), so the shareable/MCP shelf labels them attribution while the four legacy treebanks stay bare and inherit `nc`. **P13-1b (2026-07-11, shipped): `UD_Old_East_Slavic-Ruthenian` added** вҖ” the seventh treebank, `old-east-slavic-ruthenian`. "prosta mova" (Old Belarusian/Ukrainian) legal/chancery texts ca. 1380вҖ“1650 (Polotsk letters, Lithuanian Metrica, Lokhvitsa town-hall book), the THIRD East Slavic branch with zero text overlap with Birchbark/RNC/TOROT. LICENSE GATE PASSED at fixture time: `LICENSE.txt` verbatim "The treebank is licensed under the Creative Commons License Attribution-ShareAlike 4.0 International" + README machine-readable metadata `License: CC BY-SA 4.0` (GitHub license field reads `NOASSERTION`; the in-repo grant is authoritative, as for Birchbark/RNC) вҶ’ `attribution` via the same P10-4 per-document `license_override`; source class stays `nc`. Language `orv` (file-stem prefix `orv_ruthenian`; the per-doc `# lang = orv-be` is a finer BCP-47 regional subtag, not the treebank tag). Config+fixture change, no new family; dedup guard untouched. Full UD org re-check: no Old Slovene / historical South Slavic treebank exists (survey: `.docs/surveys/slavic-survey-2.md`, gitignored planning material). **P25-2 (2026-07-17, shipped): two Old Irish glosses treebanks** вҖ” the Celtic axis's UD pair (survey `.docs/surveys/celtic-survey.md`), both diplomatic-edition conversions by Adrian Doyle (NUI Galway), both test-set only, language `sga` (the glosses code-mix Latin inside Irish вҖ” the same one-tag-per-treebank honesty as RNC under `orv`). **`old-irish-dipsgg`** (`UD_Old_Irish-DipSGG`): the St Gall Priscian glosses, 3,471 glosses in the collection (the dependency-annotated test split serves 64 sentences today), converted from Bernhard Bauer's morphological analysis (stgallpriscian.ie, Moran). LICENSE GATE PASSED at fixture time 2026-07-17: `LICENSE.txt` is verbatim, in its entirety, "CC BY-NC-SA 4.0" (README metadata agrees) вҶ’ **rides the source `nc` class unchanged, no override**. **`old-irish-dipwbg`** (`UD_Old_Irish-DipWBG`): the WГјrzburg glosses on the Pauline Epistles, 42 glosses (tiny; upstream says more will be added as annotation continues), from wurzburg.ie. LICENSE verbatim: `LICENSE.txt` "The treebank is licensed under the Creative Commons License Attribution-ShareAlike 4.0 International" + README metadata `License: CC BY-SA 4.0` вҶ’ `attribution` via the same P10-4 per-document `license_override` (the birchbark/RNC mechanics); source class stays `nc`. OVERLAP NOTE, no dedup: DipSGG's text = the same St Gall glosses CorPH (P25-0) carries at a different grain (UD dependencies here, CorPH morphology there) вҖ” two honest witnesses, the MW-beside-kaikki precedent; the dedup guard exists for RE-EXPORTS of already-synced sources (chu-PROIEL/orv-TOROT), which this is not. Config+fixture change, no new family; rows flow at the next owner-fired `bin/nabu sync ud` (no per-treebank enablement exists вҖ” the `ud` source syncs its whole TREEBANKS map). **P31-0 (2026-07-19, shipped): `UD_Hittite-HitTB` added** вҖ” the tenth treebank, `hittite-hittb`, the ONE Hittite treebank in UD and the library's Anatolian entry point: 136 sentences / 1,309 words of Hoffner & Melchert tutorial examples (A Grammar of the Hittite Language, Part 2), each carrying its REAL manuscript/edition locus in `# source` (`KBo 6.2 i 16-17 (OH/OS) = Laws В§10`), spanning Old/Middle/New Hittite; test-set only (the DipWBG shape). Language `hit`. Clitic chains (`ta=an`, `nu=za`вҖҰ) arrive as CoNLL-U multiword-token ranges вҖ” 255 file-wide, the Latin-ITTB machinery exercised at scale, no parser change. LEMMA fully populated (1,309/1,309; Sumerograms lemmatized to Hittite readings, `LГҡ.U19.LU-an` вҶ’ `antuhЕЎa-`) вҶ’ `hit` joins the lemma-indexed languages. Config+fixture change, no new family. **P31-6 (2026-07-19, shipped): the Perseus pair** вҖ” `ancient-greek-perseus` (`UD_Ancient_Greek-Perseus`) + `latin-perseus` (`UD_Latin-Perseus`), treebanks eleven and twelve: the UD conversions of the native Perseus AGDT/LDT v2.1 (row 17's UD half вҖ” both READMEs verbatim: "automatic conversion of a selection of passages from the Ancient Greek and Latin Dependency Treebank 2.1"). Censused at fixture time: grc 13,919 sentences / 202,989 words (train/dev/test; Homer, Hesiod, tragedy, Herodotus, AthenaeusвҖҰ), lat 2,273 sentences / 29,223 words (train/test only, NO dev split; Vergil, Ovid, Cicero, PetroniusвҖҰ). DEDUP HONESTY: nabu has never synced the native AGLDT, so the chu-PROIEL re-export guard does not apply вҖ” no double-load; no overlap with greek-proiel/latin-ittb (different upstream data); vs the perseus-greek/latin TEXT sources these are the same works at treebank grain = distinct witnesses, never deduped (the DipSGG-beside-CorPH doctrine). LICENSE GATE PASSED at fixture time 2026-07-19: each repo's `LICENSE.txt` verbatim "This work is licensed under the Creative Commons Attribution-NonCommercial-ShareAlike 2.5 Generic License." + README metadata `License: CC BY-NC-SA 2.5` (consistent, both repos) вҶ’ NonCommercial: both ride the source `nc` class bare, **no override** (the DipSGG posture). Config+fixture change, no new family. **P32-0 (2026-07-19, shipped): the Classical Chinese pair вҖ” the Sino axis opens.** `classical-chinese-kyoto` (`UD_Classical_Chinese-Kyoto`) + `classical-chinese-tuecl` (`UD_Classical_Chinese-TueCL`), treebanks thirteen and fourteen, language `lzh` both вҖ” the library's FIRST lzh lane (SuttaCentral's 272 lzh ДҖgama roots stay scope-skipped until sibling P32-1). Kyoto (Yasuoka et al., Institute for Research in Humanities, Kyoto University; v2.18 active, changelog 2026-05-25) censused WHOLE at fixture time: **86,239 sentences / 433,169 words / 9,641 distinct lemmas** across и«–иӘһ, еӯҹеӯҗ, зҰ®иЁҳ, еҚҒе…«еҸІз•Ҙ, жҘҡиҫӯ, жҲ°еңӢзӯ–, е”җи©©дёүзҷҫйҰ– and three sutras (ж‘©иЁ¶иҲ¬иӢҘжіўзҫ…иңңеӨ§жҳҺе‘Әз¶“, йҮ‘еүӣиҲ¬иӢҘжіўзҫ…иңңз¶“, дҪӣиӘӘйҳҝеҪҢйҷҖз¶“) вҖ” ~42.2 MB of conllu, train/dev/test = +3 docs / +86,239 passages at the next owner-fired sync; LEMMA fully populated (433,169/433,169), XPOS carries the Kyoto four-field kanbun tags, MISC carries `Gloss=` English glosses. SCALE HONESTY (all thirteen sibling treebank repos censused whole upstream 2026-07-19): Kyoto alone exceeds everything the ud source has synced to date (the 2026-07-04 four-treebank first sync = 76,642 sentences) and is ~3.2x the largest existing treebank (Sanskrit-Vedic 27,182 / ITTB 26,977 next); it does NOT exceed the combined 107,664-sentence thirteen-treebank registry but grows it by +80% in one bite вҖ” the loud sync-delta note lives in sources.yml. TueCL (TГјbingen: Chen, Wang, ГҮГ¶ltekin; since v2.14) is the 100-sentence / 648-word Zhuangzi йҖҚйҒҘжёё rider, test-set only (the DipWBG shape) = +1 doc / +100 passages; its free-form no-`=` working-note comments (bare Chinese notes, `# ???вҖҰ` annotator questions) ride through the parser ignored вҖ” only sent_id/text/source are interpreted. Neither corpus has MWT ranges or empty nodes file-wide (character-per-word, no clitic fusion вҖ” checked across all splits). **LICENSE GATE PASSED at fixture time 2026-07-19 WITH A RECORDED DISCREPANCY:** Kyoto's `LICENSE.txt` is verbatim "The treebank is licensed under the Creative Commons License Attribution-ShareAlike 4.0 International" but its README machine-readable metadata says **`License: PD`** вҖ” a substantive PD-vs-BY-SA fork, not a version slip. Ruling: LICENSE.txt authoritative (the Ruthenian NOASSERTION precedent вҖ” the in-repo grant governs; and BY-SA is the conservative reading, it can never over-share) вҶ’ `attribution` via the P10-4 per-document `license_override`. TueCL's `LICENSE.txt` is byte-identical BY-SA 4.0 and its README AGREES (`License: CC BY-SA 4.0`) вҶ’ same override; source class stays `nc`. No re-export guard concern (neither converts a source nabu syncs); breaker rebalance re-derived at fourteen (minimum tripping count stays 3: 3 > 0.2Г—14 = 2.8). JOURNAL: `UD_Old_Japanese-LMJ` NOT taken вҖ” misnamed (its material is Heike/LMJ-era, not Old Japanese) and its master branch is EMPTY of data (verified 2026-07-19: only CONTRIBUTING.md, LICENSE.txt, template README вҖ” no .conllu); Old Japanese arrives via ONCOJ (row 97, P32-2); if LMJ master ever gains data it is a fresh license-gate decision, not a config flip. Config+fixture change, no new family. **P33-3 (2026-07-20, shipped): the KyotoвҶ”Kanripo crosswalk вҖ” producer #8 `Nabu::KyotoKanripoCrosswalk` on the `reference_producer` seam (row 104's treebankвҶ”corpus bridge).** The Kyoto treebank's own `# newdoc id` lines ARE the id map (censused WHOLE upstream 2026-07-20: **all 936 newdoc ids across the three splits are `<KR-id>_<juan>` вҖ” ten distinct texts**; the README's per-split text listing is stale against the data вҖ” it swaps the dev/train sutras (data: KR6f0082 in dev, KR6c0023 in train) вҖ” newdoc ids authoritative): и«–иӘһ KR1h0004 (20 juan-docs) В· еӯҹеӯҗ KR1h0001 (14) В· зҰ®иЁҳ KR1d0052 (50) В· еҚҒе…«еҸІз•Ҙ KR2b0041 (19) В· жҲ°еңӢзӯ– KR2e0003 (501) В· жҘҡиҫӯ KR4a0001 (9) В· е”җи©©дёүзҷҫйҰ– KR4h0169 (320) В· the three sutras KR6c0127/KR6c0023/KR6f0082 (1 each). Document-grain kind=`reference` edges split-file вҶ” `urn:nabu:kanripo:<KR-id>` (detail = firstвҖҰlast newdoc span + exact juan count), re-derived from the canonical conllu after every `ud` sync вҖ” the P32-6 canonical-file producer contract: a workdir without the kyoto treebank (true until the owner-fired P32-0 sync) is a no-op that supersedes nothing; at the real sync, 3 split files Г— their texts = **22 edges**. COVERAGE: wave-1 KR1/KR3/KR4 resolves **5 of 10 texts (413/936 newdocs, 44%)**; KR2b0041 + KR2e0003 (520 newdocs, 56%) resolve at the P33-1 KR2 wave; the three KR6 sutras stay dangling under the KR6-exclusion doctrine (CBETA row 105 is the Buddhist shelf) вҖ” all minted anyway, dangling-but-stable (the P32-6 precedent). CAVEAT censused 2026-07-20: **KR4h0169 is in NEITHER the KR-Catalog (KR4h ends at 0168) nor the kanripo org (repo 404)** вҖ” a Kyoto-local extension of the id space (their ud-kanbun GitLab hosts `kanripo/kR4h0169`; same Kyoto IRH id authority) вҖ” minted like the rest, dangling until Kanripo publishes it. TueCL carries NO Kanripo ids (bare numeric sent_ids, no newdoc lines) вҶ’ no edges, the edge-worthiness rule. Fixture: `lzh_kyoto-ud-dev-slices.conllu` (six real newdoc runs, five texts across wave-1/KR2/KR6); the и«–иӘһ edge pinned end-to-end (producer вҶ’ journal вҶ’ `Query::Links` with both catalog sides loaded). **P40-1 (Germanic axis / Icelandic IcePaHC, shipped):** the `TREEBANKS` map grew to **15 treebanks** вҖ” **`icelandic-icepahc`** (`UD_Icelandic-IcePaHC`, a rule-based UD conversion of the Icelandic Parsed Historical Corpus; `CC BY-SA 4.0`, LICENSE.txt + README metadata agree, verified 2026-07-22 вҶ’ per-document `attribution` override, source class stays `nc`). **Diachronic honesty (stated, not hidden):** the corpus spans the **12thвҖ“21st century** (Old Norse sagas to modern prose) yet UD files the whole thing under the ONE modern ISO 639 tag **`is`** вҖ” the same one-tag-per-treebank practice as RNC's Middle Russian under `orv` (P10-2), carried verbatim. Config+fixture change, no new family; the head-50 dev-split fixture exercises exactly one multiword-token range (`1-2 lГЎttu` вҶ’ `lГЎt`+`ГҫГә`) on the ITTB MWT path. `is` is the library's first Icelandic language lane. Arrives at the owner's next `bin/nabu sync ud` (`ud` already enabled; no per-treebank enablement exists). See `test/fixtures/ud/README.md`. |
| 5 | **TOROT (TromsГё OCS & Old Russian Treebank)** | OCS + Old East Slavic, lemmatized | PROIEL XML / CoNLL-U | 3 | 5 | 4 | 5 | Directly serves the Slavic research axis. Shares PROIEL adapter. **Status: LIVE** вҖ” first sync 2026-07-04: 40 docs incl. Zographensis, 0 quarantined. |
| 6 | **GRETIL** | Vast Sanskrit (+ Pali, Prakrit, TibetanвҖҰ) e-texts | TEI P5 XML (mass-converted), legacy HTML/text | 5 | 2 | 3 | 3 (CC BY-NC-SA 4.0, `nc`) | **Status: READY (P9-4b + P9-4c + P10-3 recovery, 2026-07-09) вҖ” adapter + `gretil` parser family shipped, `enabled: false` awaiting owner-fired first sync.** Current corpus = mass-converted TEI P5 (**784** XML texts, ~240 MB; fetched via the shared git path from the byte-identical GitHub mirror `mmehner/gretil-corpus-tei@master` вҖ” mirror-scope verified: its 784 XML = the live `corpustei/` count, GRETIL's TEI conversion stable since 2021). **NOT EpiDoc** вҖ” no `refsDecl`, no CTS: a new bespoke parser family (`GretilParser`), not EpidocParser reuse. Four addressability rungs handled: (a) attribute-cited `div[@n]`/`lg[@xml:id]`/`l[@n]` вҶ’ citation = `l/@n` verbatim (e.g. `1.001.01a`), lg/div as annotation context; (b) in-text `// BrbUp_N //` verse markers (the marker closes the verse it follows; stripped from the passage, its number the citation); (c) unaddressed prose вҶ’ `pN` ordinals, flagged non-canonical; **(d, P9-4c) pure `lg[@xml:id]` citation** (`<lg xml:id="RgV_1.1.1">` вҶ’ `1.1.1`, prefix stripped), a fallback pass run only when (a)/(b)/(c) leave the doc empty. **P9-4c quarantine recovery (118 вҶ’ ~0):** the P9-4b first sync quarantined 118/781 files in two classes, recovered by (1) the xml:id rung above (~60 "no-citable" pure-`lg[@xml:id]` files вҖ” RДҒmДҒyaб№Үa, Buddhacarita, GД«tagovinda, KirДҒtДҒrjunД«ya, вҖҰ); (2) a single-pipe marker variant `| BBs_1,1.1 |` (~13 files вҖ” also a fallback pass, so already-loaded docs that merely contain `| вҖҰ |` reading text stay untouched); (3) collision tolerance вҖ” a duplicate citation no longer quarantines the document but disambiguates deterministically (`:b2`, `:b3`, вҖҰ in document order; the ddbdp precedent), plus a **multi-prefix join** for interleaved kДҒrikДҒ/commentary (вүҘ2 marker prefixes whose bare numbers collide вҶ’ `DhvK.1.1` vs `DhvA.1.1`). **P10-3 residue micro-packet (quarantines 8 вҶ’ 4):** the P9-4c census left 8 quarantined вҖ” 4 genuinely unaddressable flat `<lg>`/`<l>` lists (`sa_abhinavagupta-paramArthasAra`, `sa_bIjanighaNTu`, `sa_lagadha-RgvedavedAGgajyotiSa`, `sa_vAmadeva-janmamaraNavicAra` вҖ” zero `@n`/xml:id/marker/prose, stay quarantined by design) + 4 recoverable **line-terminated marker** files whose marker sits at the END of an `<l>`, terminated by the `</l>` boundary rather than a closing delimiter: (a) hyphenated closed `// Abhidh-d_N //` (`sa_vimalamitra-abhidharmadIpa`; the primary `// Abbr_N //` prefix charset excludes the hyphen) and (b) leading-`//`-only `// Abbr_N</l>` (`sa_sAtvatatantra`, `sa_somAnanda-zAktavijJAna`, `sa_puruSottamadeva-ekAkSarakoza`; no closing `//`). Both recovered by a `LINE_MARKER` regex (hyphen-admitting prefix, optional closing `//`, `\z`-anchored) applied per `<l>` in a `LineMarkerExtraction` pass run LAST вҖ” only when the primary/xml:id/pipe passes leave the doc empty, so the two existing marker regexes stay byte-identical. Frozen-urn guard held: all 663 (P9-4c) / 773 (P10-3) previously-clean docs re-parse byte-identical (read-only two-parse census). IAST (`sa-Latn` вҶ’ `san-Latn`), NFC. Vedic accents ride in **bare `<orig>`** (combining U+0331/U+030D) вҖ” policy KEEPS `<orig>` (pristine accented text) and DROPS any paired `<reg>`, the INVERSE of DdbdpParser's Leiden rule. License uniformly **CC BY-NC-SA 4.0** вҶ’ `license_class: nc`, under an aggregator takedown disclaimer; ingestable for local research, kept out of the P8-1 MCP surface and any redistribution. urn `urn:nabu:gretil:<literal-filename-slug>:<citation>`. **P11-7 (silent strays, 2026-07-10):** two genuine editions вҖ” `sa_vijJAnezvara-mitAkSarA` (the 1.8 MB MitДҒkб№ЈarДҒ, 4788 prose passages) and `sa_haribhadrasUri-zAstravArttAsamuccaya` (701 xml:id verses) вҖ” carry a `<text>` with NO `@xml:lang` (their teiHeader `xml:lang="en"` describes the metadata, not the edition), so `peek_header` returned nil and discovery dropped them INVISIBLY (not even quarantined вҖ” never counted). Language now falls back to `<body>/@xml:lang` (`sa-Latn` вҶ’ `san-Latn`, the accurate corpus form), then the filename `sa_` prefix вҖ” recovering both (+2 docs, live). The 4 P10-3-residue flat-`lg` files stay quarantined by design (unchanged). Systemic: `Gretil#discovery_skips` now makes any non-edition XML a VISIBLE skip count, never a silent drop. |
| 7 | **Digital Corpus of Sanskrit (DCS)** (Oliver Hellwig) | Gold-lemmatized Sanskrit corpus: **15,900 CoNLL-U chapter files / 270 texts / ~844 MB, ~5.46M analyzed words** (readme census), IAST | **Standard CoNLL-U** (UD-compliant since the Aug 2022 release), living at `dcs/data/conllu/` **inside `github.com/OliverHellwig/sanskrit`** вҖ” this row previously named a nonexistent "dcs-data" repo and a "custom text format"; both CORRECTED at P26-0 fixture time (2026-07-18, commit `04e0778d`) | 4 | 5 | 5 | 5 (CC BY 4.0) | Every token analyzed вҖ” the analysis-side complement to GRETIL's breadth, and the first **gold Sanskrit** occupant of the lemma index. License **verbatim in both data readmes** fetched with the corpus: `dcs/data/conllu/readme.md` "The data in this directory are licensed under the Creative Commons BY 4.0 (CC BY 4.0) license." + `dcs/data/readme.md` "The data of the DCS and any data in child directories are licensed under the Creative Common BY 4.0 (CC BY 4.0) license." (citation requested: Hellwig, *The Digital Corpus of Sanskrit*, 2010вҖ“2024). **GOLD IS MACHINE-DECLARED**: `lookup/chapter-info.xml` carries `<layer type="gold">lexicon</layer>` + `<layer type="gold">morpho-syntax</layer>` for **all 15,900 chapters** (census 2026-07-18; 1,780 add gold `syntax` вҖ” the Vedic Treebank subset, the only chapters with filled HEAD/DEPREL), corroborated by the readme's "The analysis of each string has been verified by one annotator" вҖ” the adapter GATES its gold claim on the declaration (undeclared/non-gold chapter вҶ’ quarantine) and never touches the 7,227 automatic `.conllu_parsed` sibling files. **Status: READY (P26-0, 2026-07-18)** вҖ” `Dcs` adapter on the conllu family: document per chapter file (the corpus's own unit), passage per sentence, urns from upstream's permanent numeric ids (`urn:nabu:dcs:<textId>:<chapterId>:<sent_id>`); chapter metadata (text/chapter names, position, time slot, Vedic `<details>` register/veda вҶ’ facets) rides the document; MISC `LemmaId`/`OccId`/`Unsandhied` ride the tokens verbatim. Fetch = the P26-0 **sparse GitFetch** (blobless no-checkout clone + sparse cone `dcs/data/conllu` + parent readme) so the owner's first sync materializes the ~844 MB cone, not the ~1.7 GB repo. Open data = **ORACC JSON**, delivered as a per-project **zip over HTTP** at `https://oracc.museum.upenn.edu/json/<project>.zip` (subprojects hyphenated: `saao-saa01.zip`); `application/zip` + `Last-Modified` for change detection. **NO git data repo** (`oracc/publicdata` empty, `oracc/json` 404) вҶ’ the six existing adapters' git-clone `fetch` does **not** apply; ORACC needs a **new HTTP-zip fetch path** (the first non-git fetcher). Each `corpusjson/<id>.json` is a nested **`cdl` tree** (`c` chunk / `d` discontinuity / `l` lemma): a transliteration line reconstructs by concatenating `l`-node `form` fragments between `line-start` `d`-nodes, tracking `surface` d-nodes (obverse/reverse) and line numbers вҖ” determinatives (`{ki}`, `{d}`), subscript numerals (`ZIвӮғ`), and ЕЎ/б№Ј/б№ӯ preserved. Every `l`-node carries **gold lemmatization**: `form` (translit) В· `norm` (normalization) В· `cf` (lemma/citation form) В· `gw`+`sense` (English gloss) В· `pos`/`epos` вҖ” the `annotations_json` lemma-search goldmine (P7-5 path reuses it). **Prose translations are NOT in the JSON** (0 translation nodes across 265 SAA texts) вҖ” and no public bulk artifact carries them (P13-4 Phase A: `oracc/catf` on GitHub is C-ATF transliteration-only, 0 `#tr` lines, stale 2019; per-text `.atf`/`.xtf`/`_project-en.json` endpoints are soft-404s вҖ” a 200 whose body is `404\n` вҖ” on every mirror). **P13-4 (owner-approved 2026-07-11, "Two-stage SAA-first crawl"): the running English IS ingested** вҖ” crawled from the official per-text fragment `/<project>/<textid>/html` (CORS-open; a typical SAA letter вүҲ 55 KB), whose translation cells carry the SAME node refs as the corpusjson `line-start` d-nodes, giving mechanical unitвҶ”line alignment. `OraccTranslationParser` mints one `-en` sibling document per translated text (`urn:nabu:oracc:<project>:<P/Q>-en`, one passage per translation UNIT at its anchor line's label вҖ” SAA units are paragraph-grained: 39 lines / 6 units in SAA 01 175), and `Query::Parallel` gained the ORACC work pattern, so `show <tablet-urn> --parallel` span-groups tablet lines under their English blocks exactly like the card-cited Homers (MCP `nabu_show parallel: true` likewise). License verbatim (kijyunn.html): гҖҢгғ•гӮЎгӮӨгғ«гҒҜгҖҒжңүе„ҹгғ»з„Ўе„ҹгҒ§гҒӮгӮӢгҒӢгӮ’е•ҸгӮҸгҒҡгҖҒиҮӘз”ұгҒ«иӨҮиЈҪгғ»еҶҚй…Қеёғгғ»е…ұжңүгҒҷгӮӢгҒ“гҒЁгҒҢгҒ§гҒҚгҒҫгҒҷгҖӮгҖҚ вҶ’ class `open` (the survey's "public_domain" label; the vulgate precedent), еә•жң¬ attribution requested and carried as metadata. The sign-the-CCAT-declaration route is accordingly DOUBTFUL: the rights holder locates the database's licensing with Accordance, so do not sign-and-ingest without revisiting. Remaining honest paths: Swete 1909 (already held) or STEPBible's planned TAGOT. **P26-4 footnote вҖ” the lineage resurfaces:** the Diorisis corpus (#69) ships 53 Septuagint files (`tlgAuthor 0527`, via Bibliotheca Augustana вҖ” Rahlfs-lineage; scout text-diffed divergent from held Swete); its adapter EXCLUDES them by the machine-readable header field вҖ” another Rahlfs dead end, skipped by rule, never ingested. |
| 47 | **GORAZD вҖ” Old Church Slavonic Digital Hub** (gorazd.org, Institute of Slavonic Studies, Czech Academy) | The digitized Prague **SJS** (*SlovnГӯk jazyka staroslovДӣnskГ©ho*, the most comprehensive OCS dictionary in existence, ~33k entries) + Cejtlin *Staroslavjanskij slovar'* + GreekвҖ“OCS index + card archive. **NB: Miklosich and Sreznevsky are NOT in the hub** (packet lead corrected) | **SURVEYED-BLOCKED (P13-1, 2026-07-11).** Query-only web UI (Gulliver); no download, no API, and **no content license anywhere** вҖ” only GDPR/cookie text; the advertised GNU GPL covers the *software tools*, not the data. No LINDAT/CLARIAH-CZ deposit (the ASEP CC0 covers catalog metadata only). The unlicensed GitHub scrape `utajum/old-church-slavonic-dictionary` (33,036 records, GORAZD ids in the JSON) proves the data is structured (per-entry Greek/Latin equivalents + 5-language glosses) but inherits the block вҖ” never ingest it without the grant. Unblock: data-sharing agreement with the SlovanskГҪ Гәstav AV ДҢR вҖ” the highest-value Slavic dictionary unblock there is. See `.docs/surveys/slavic-survey-2.md`. |
| 48 | **Miklosich, *Lexicon palaeoslovenico-graeco-latinum* вҖ” BCDH/ELEXIS TEI edition** | The 1862вҖ“65 OCSвҖ“GreekвҖ“Latin lexicon (PD by age), **41,338 entries**, converted to TEI (Lex-0) by the Belgrade Center for Digital Humanities (2022) | **SURVEYED-BLOCKED (P13-1, 2026-07-11) вҖ” the nearest dictionary-shelf prize.** CLARIN.si record 11356/1666 is **metadata-only**: 0 downloadable files, no `dc:rights` (verified on the record page; REST `"bitstreams":[]`). If released it would drop into the **existing TEI dictionary adapter family** вҖ” no new format work. Unblock: email BCDH/ELEXIS (or repo-help@clarin.si) to complete the deposit + confirm license. PD scans (archive.org, MDZ) remain the OCR fallback. See `.docs/surveys/slavic-survey-2.md`. |
| 49 | **South Slavic Church Slavonic editions: Croatian (Staroslavenski institut) В· Serbian (SANU) В· Bulgarian (Cyrillomethodiana/histdict, Sofia) В· DIACU (CNR)** | Croatian: RCJHR dictionary (letters AвҖ“I) + 60-source Glagolitic corpus; Serbian: 12thвҖ“18th c. corpus, ~450k-word medieval slice, morph-annotated; Bulgarian: ~147 texts 10thвҖ“18th c. + *StarobДғlgarski reДҚnik*; DIACU: 652-doc diachronic ChSl JSON (22.8 MB) | **SURVEYED-BLOCKED (P13-1, 2026-07-11) вҖ” no open machine-readable South Slavic ChSl edition exists.** Croatian: dictionary is **scanned-page PDFs**, corpus unpublished, no license (unblock: write info@stin.hr). Serbian: internal to the SANU dictionary project, no release (unblock: contact the Institute for the Serbian Language). Bulgarian: web-UI only, footer verbatim "В© РЎРҫС„РёР№СҒРәРё СғРҪРёРІРөСҖСҒРёСӮРөСӮ вҖһРЎРІ. РҡР»РёРјРөРҪСӮ РһС…СҖРёРҙСҒРәРё" 2011-2022" вҖ” no grant (unblock: ask the Sofia team). DIACU (`MariaCassese/DIACU`): clean JSON but **no LICENSE file** (GitHub `license: null`) and the OCS core is re-packaged TOROT/PROIEL already held (sampled Zographensis record sources `torottreebank/treebank-releases`) вҖ” only the New-ChSl/Ruthenian slices are novel (unblock: ask the author; low value net of overlap). Adjacent but open: **CroALa** вҖ” Croatian **Latin**, ~5.6M words TEI, CC-BY, GitHub+Zenodo вҖ” noted for a future Latin-breadth phase. See `.docs/surveys/slavic-survey-2.md`. |

## Ranking synthesis

**By effort-to-value (build order):** 1 вҶ’ 2 вҶ’ 4 вҶ’ 3/5 вҶ’ 10 вҶ’ 7 вҶ’ 8 вҶ’ 11 вҶ’ 6 вҶ’ 9 вҶ’ 15 вҶ’ 14 вҶ’ 18/19 вҶ’ 13.

Rationale: adapters 1вҖ“2 share one EpiDoc/CTS implementation and immediately deliver the classical backbone; 3вҖ“5 share the PROIEL/CoNLL-U implementation and deliver the annotated IE layer; 10 reuses EpiDoc. That's three parser families covering ten sources. TITUS (#13) is deliberately late despite top-tier content: it's the highest-friction integration and should be attempted only once the normalization layer is mature enough to absorb its encoding chaos.

**By content criticality for the Slavic/IE research axis:** 3, 5, 19, 18, 13, 4 вҖ” these are the corpora whose absence would actually block work.

**By licensing cleanliness (safe to ever share/publish derivatives):** 1, 2, 7, 8, 9, 10, 15, 16 (CC with attribution) > 3, 5 (NC clause) > 6, 14, 19 (research-use, keep private) > 13, 23вҖ“27 (private use only, segregate).

**Format families вҶ’ shared parser components:**
- *EpiDoc/CTS TEI:* Perseus, First1KGreek, Papyri.info
- *PROIEL XML:* PROIEL, TOROT
- *CoNLL-U:* UD, DCS (native since Aug 2022), AGDT
- *ATF/JSON:* ORACC, CDLI
- *Bespoke:* GRETIL, TITUS, Sefaria JSON, ETCSL, TLA, kanripo, CCMH
- *IIIF image feeds (вҶ’ HTR):* e-codices, ADA, DigiVatLib (see unlockables)
